Note from TSB

                      Approval and deletion of ITU-T Recommendations
By AAP-12, it was announced that the following ITU-T Recommendations were approved, in accordance with the
procedures outlined in Recommendation ITU-T A.8:
–       ITU-T K.114 (08/2022): Electromagnetic compatibility requirements and measurement methods for digital
        cellular mobile communication base station equipment
–       ITU-T Y.4052 (08/2022): Vocabulary for blockchain for supporting Internet of things and smart cities and
        communities in data processing and management aspects
–       ITU-T Y.4216 (08/2022): Requirements of sensing and data collection system for city infrastructure
–       ITU-T Y.4217 (08/2022): Service requirements and capability framework for IoT-related crowdsourced
        systems
–       ITU-T Y.4481 (08/2022): Framework for data middle-platform in IoT and smart sustainable cities
–       ITU-T Y.4482 (08/2022): Requirements and framework for smart livestock farming based on the Internet of
        things
–       ITU-T Y.4483 (08/2022): Reference architecture of service exposure for decentralized services for Internet
        of things applications
–       ITU-T Y.4484 (08/2022): Framework to support Web of Objects ontology based semantic data
        interoperability of eHealth services
–       ITU-T Y.4600 (08/2022): Requirements and capabilities of a digital twin system for smart cities



By TSB Circular 35 of 1 September 2022, it was announced that the following ITU-T Recommendations were
deleted, in accordance with the procedures outlined in Resolution 1:
–       ITU-T D.280 (03/1995): Principles for charging and billing, accounting and reimbursements for universal
        personal telecommunication
–       ITU-T E.168 (05/2002): Application of E.164 numbering plan for UPT
–       ITU-T E.168.1 (02/2005): Assignment procedures for universal personal telecommunications (UPT)
        numbers in the provisioning of the international UPT service
–       ITU-T E.174 (04/1995): Routing principles and guidance for Universal Personal Telecommunications (UPT)
–       ITU-T E.755 (02/1996): Reference connections for UPT traffic performance and GOS
–       ITU-T E.775 (02/1996): UPT grade of service concept
–       ITU-T E.776 (10/1996): Network grade of service parameters for UPT
–       ITU-T F.850 (03/1993): Principles of Universal Personal Telecommunication (UPT)
–       ITU-T F.851 (02/1995): Universal Personal Telecommunication (UPT) – Service description (service set 1)
–       ITU-T F.852 (03/2000): Universal Personal Telecommunication (UPT) – Service description (service set 2)
–       ITU-T F.853 (11/1998): Supplementary services in the Universal Personal Telecommunication (UPT)
        environment




                International Public Telecommunication Numbering Plan
                            (Recommendation ITU-T E.164)
Note from TSB
At the request of the Administration of the State of Palestine and according to Recommendations ITU-T E.164 and
E.164.1, the Director of TSB has assigned the Country Code “970” to the State of Palestine. The activation date of
the Country Code 970 and the transition plan to the new Country Code (970) will be advised later.


Note from TSB
The country code “878”, previously assigned for the provision of Universal Personal Telecommunications (UPT)
global service, is returned to spare.


Note from TSB
                  Number Series for international Universal Personal Telecommunications (UPT)

Associated with shared country code 878 for international UPT service, the following UPT number series have been
withdrawn:

                             Mobile Country or Geographical Area Codes
                                  (Recommendation ITU-T E.212)
Note from TSB
At the request of the Administration of the State of Palestine, the Director of TSB has assigned the Mobile Country
Code (MCC) 423, for the mobile networks of the State of Palestine in accordance with Recommendation ITU-T E.212.

Faroe Islands (country code +298)
Communication of 15.VIII.2022:
The Telecommunication Authority of the Faroe Islands (FTA), Tórshavn, announces that the operator Tosa Sp/f
(Company Reg. No. 6724) has ceased operations. The company has, as per 15 August 2022, handed back to the FTA
its authorization as telecommunications provider according to the Faroese Telecommunications Act section 4 and
has handed back the assigned number-series "+298 91xxxx". Furthermore, the FTA has revoked the allocation of
MCC+MNC 288 03 to Tosa Sp/f.
Simultaneously, the FTA wishes to notify the ITU of the reassignment on 15 August 2022 of the "+298 91xxxx"
numbering series for GSM Mobile Services to operator P/F FT Samskifti, Klingran 3, FO-188 Hoyvík, Faroe Islands
(Company Reg. No. 3980). FT Samskifti is a member of the Faroese Telecom Group (www.ft.fo).
The assignment of numbers can be consulted on the following Faroese Telecommunication Authority web page
(see file Nummarætlan.xls): http://www.fjarskiftiseftirlitid.fo/fo/fjarskifti/nummarskipan/

Contact:
       Telecommunication Authority of the Faroe Islands
       Skálatrøð 20, P.O. Box 73,
       FO-110 Tórshavn
       Faroe Islands
       Tel:     +298 35 60 20
       Fax:     +298 35 60 35
       E-mail: fjarskiftiseftirlitid@vs.fo
       URL: www.fjarskiftiseftirlitid.fo




Germany (country code +49)
Communication of 25.VIII.2022:

Railway, Mainz, announces the National Numbering Plan for Germany:

Presentation of E.164 National Numbering Plan for country code +49 (Germany):

a) General Survey:           Minimum number length (excluding country code):                   3 digits
                             Maximum number length (excluding country code):                  13 digits
                             (Exceptions: IVPN (NDC 181):                                     14 digits
                                          Paging Services (NDC 168, 169):                     14 digits)

Kazakhstan (country code +7)
Communication of 1.VI.2022:
The Ministry of Digital Development, Innovations and Aerospace Industry of the Republic of Kazakhstan, Nur-Sultan,
announces the national numbering plan of Kazakhstan.

General Information:

1. The capital of the Republic of Kazakhstan is Nur-Sultan city
2. Time Zone: UTC+6
3. The country code of Kazakhstan is +7
4. The international number consists of eleven (11) digits.

The Republic of Kazakhstan consists of seventeen (17) area units with following nominations:
                             Area unit                                         Centre of area
          Nur-Sultan city of republican significance              Nur-Sultan
          Almaty city of republican significance                  Almaty
          Shymkent city of republican significance                Shymkent
          Aqmola Area                                         Kokshetau
          Almaty Area                                         Taldykorgan
          Aqtobe Area                                         Aqtobe
          Atyrau Area                                         Atyrau
          Qostanai Area                                       Qostanai
          Qaragandy Area                                      Qaragandy

          Zhambyl Area                                        Taraz

                  Status of radiocommunications between
                   amateur stations of different countries
(in accordance with optional provision No. 25.1 of the Radio Regulations) and
             Form of call signs assigned by each administration
                  to its amateur and experimental stations
                            (Annex to ITU Operational Bulletin No. 1251 – 1.IX.2022)
                                             (Amendment No. 1)

P 12 Austria


Amateur stations:                         OE followed by a digit 1-9, indicating the province or the area in
                                          which the station is located and by a suffix of 2, 3 or 4 letters
                                          Only 1-letter indicating contest stations, limited and temporarily
                                          licensed, explicit for club stations
                                          Suffix first letter: “X” indicating beacon, relays and club stations;
                                          “Q” is not possible

Experimental stations:                    OE followed by a digit (2-9, indicating the province in which the
                                          station is situated) and by 2 letters (QA-QZ)

Digits indicating the provinces
  or areas:
                                          1 – Vienna (amateur stations only)
                                          2 – Salzburg
                                          3 – Lower Austria and Vienna (experimental stations only)
                                          4 – Burgenland
                                          5 – Upper Austria
                                          6 – Styria
                                          7 – Tyrol
                                          8 – Carinthia
                                          9 – Vorarlberg
                                          0 – exterritorial


Accordingly added letters to the
 end of the call sign:
                                          / M – mobile operation
                                          / P – portable operation
                                          / MM – on board ships
                                          / AM – on board aircrafts

                                    National Numbering Plan
                     (According to Recommendation ITU-T E.129 (01/2013))
                                          Web: www.itu.int/itu-t/inr/nnp/index.html
Administrations are requested to notify ITU about their national numbering plan changes, or to give an
explanation on their webpage concerning the national numbering plan as well as their contact points, so that the
information, which will be made available freely to all administrations/ROAs and service providers, can be posted
on the ITU-T website.
For their numbering website, or when sending their information to ITU/TSB (e-mail: tsbtson@itu.int),
administrations are kindly requested to use the format as explained in Recommendation ITU-T E.129. They are
reminded that they will be responsible for the timely update of this information.
From 15.VIII.2022, the following countries/geographical areas have updated their national numbering plan on
our site:


                             Country/ Geographical area                      Country Code (CC)
                  Morocco                                                             +212
